msg:Family travel, 4 people (three adults and one child) booked a private hot spring suite, including 3 breakfasts.
There is a double bed and a sofa bed in the house, and we added an extra single bed (with a breakfast).
The room environment is very good and clean, and there is a swing in the yard. At the same time, a canopy is set up, which is really considerate. You can also sit outside and soak in the hot spring when it rains.
Four hot spring tickets were also given when checking in, and I went to experience it. There are many pools, and there is also a ladies' area. Drinking a glass of ice milk after the hot spring is so comfortable.
Each room has an exclusive butler for one-to-one service. Our butler is Bao Rumeng, absolutely five-star praise! From the demand for supplies to the surrounding travel recommendations, they will respond patiently. Every afternoon, the options for goodnight drinks will be confirmed in advance, and the staff will be arranged to deliver them on time. The brother who delivers drinks and the lady in charge of room management are also very good.
Due to the cloudy weather in the room, the water will have a bit of an off-flavor. The lady in charge of room service is very experienced and helped us solve the problem and added a fragrance machine in the house.
The dishes in the Chinese restaurant are also delicious, the fish is fresh and tender, and the meat is firm and not loose.
I will choose here again when I come to Ningbo next time. From the state of each staff member, I can feel that the a**osphere here is very good and makes people feel happy.

Thank you to every staff member who helped us during the two days of stay.
